	          const template = createTemplate(htmlString)
	          $container.append(template)
	          const render = template.querySelector("img");
	          render.addEventListener("load",(event)=>{
	            event.srcElement.classList.add("fadeIn");
	          })
	          eventClick(template);
	        });
	      }
	      
	      const $modal = document.querySelector("#modal");
	      const $overlay = document.querySelector("#overlay");
	      const $hideModal = document.querySelector("#hide-modal");

	      const $modalImage = $modal.querySelector("img");
	      const $modalDescription = $modal.querySelector("p");
	    
	      function findById(list, id){
	        debugger
	        return list.find(movie => movie.id === parseInt(id,10))
	      }
	    
	      function findMovie(id, category){
	        switch(category){
	          case "Accion": {
	            return findById(actionList,id);
	          }
	    
	          case "Drama": {
	            return findById(dramaList,id);
	          }
	    
	          default: {
	            return findById(animationList,id);
	          }
	        }
	        
	      }
	    
	      function showModal($element){
	        $overlay.classList.add("active")
	        $modal.style.animation = "modalIn .8s forwards";
	        const id = $element.dataset.id;
	        const category = $element.dataset.category;
	        const data = findMovie(id, category);
	    
	        $modalTitle.textContent = data.title;
	        $modalImage.setAttribute("src",data.medium_cover_image); 
	        $modalDescription.textContent = data.description_full;
	    
	      }
	    
	      $hideModal.addEventListener("click",()=>{
	        $overlay.classList.remove("active")
	        $modal.style.animation = "modalOut forwards";
	      })
	    
	    })()
	    
	```

## 0210. LocalStorage

### Descripci√≥n:


### Comentarios:

* **Sergio Minei** (23)

	
	## Guardar datos
	
	  * `localStorage` permite almacenar datos sin tiempo de expiraci√≥n
	  * `sessionStorage` permite almacenar datos. Estos datos se van a borrar cuando se termine la sessi√≥n del navegador
	
	
	
	En local storage solo se puede guardar texto plano. No se pueden guardar objetos.
	``` 
	    //eliminar los datos
	    window.localStorage.clear();
	    
	    //setear un valor
	    window.localStorage.setItem("nombre", "Toshi");
	    
	    //setear un objeto
	    //primero se tiene que convertir el objeto en un string
	    window.localStorage.setItem("objeto", JSON.stringify({"peli": "wonder woman"});
	    
	    //obtener el valor de un key
	    window.localStorage.getItem("nombre");
	    
	    //obtener el valor de un texto objeto y convertirlo a objeto
	    JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("objeto"));
	    
	```
	
	Si quieren ver el resumen completo del curso lo pueden ver [aqu√≠](https://github.com/MineiToshio/CursosPlatzi/tree/master/Curso%20de%20jQuery%20a%20JavaScript). Lo ir√© actualizando a medida que vaya avanzando con el curso.

* **heysoypaez** (7)

	
	 _JSON es el brujo que hace √∫til y relevante localStorage permitiendo guardar objetos en memoria como strings y recuperarlos como objetos_
	``` 
	    //haciendo un objeto de la vida ...
	    let laVida = {
	    tristezas: 5,
	    alegrias: 10,
	    anecdotas: 8
	    }
	    
	    //convirtiendo ese objeto a json
	    laVida = JSON.stringify(laVida)
	    
	    localStorage.setItem("laVida",laVida)
	    
	    recuperando ese objeto
	    
	    localStorage.getItem("laVida")
	    laVida = JSON.parse(laVida)
	    
	    
	```

	joooooer como cuando te das cuenta que platzi graba en localStorage todos tus comentarios y los tiempos de la √∫ltima reproducci√≥n de los √∫ltimos videos

	* **Facundo Nicol√°s Garc√≠a Martoni (Platzi)** (1)
![](https://img.elcomercio.pe/files/article_content_ec_fotos/uploads/2018/12/07/5c0ade654a7cc.jpeg)

* **pablojorgeandres** (5)

	
	## [LocalStorage](https://github.com/pablojorgeandres/notas-clases/blob/master/jQuery-JavaScript.md#clase21)
	
	Para respaldar los datos que pedimos a la API utilizamos [_**localStorage**_](https://developer.mozilla.org/es/docs/Web/API/Window/localStorage) √≥ [_**sessionStorage**_](https://developer.mozilla.org/es/docs/Web/API/Window/localStorage). Son objetos nativos en javascript.
	
	[_**localStorage**_](https://developer.mozilla.org/es/docs/Web/API/Window/localStorage) nos permite guardar los datos sin un tiempo de expiraci√≥n, es decir persisten entre ventanas/tabs con el mismo origen incluso al cerrar el navegador.
	
	[_**sessionStorage**_](https://developer.mozilla.org/es/docs/Web/API/Window/localStorage) nos permite guardar los datos con tiempo de expiraci√≥n. Son eliminados cuando finaliza la sesion de navegaci√≥n, lo que ocurre cuando se cierra el navegador.
	
	[_**localStorage**_](https://developer.mozilla.org/es/docs/Web/API/Window/localStorage) es un objeto dentro de window.
	
	Para acceder:
	``` 
	    	window.localStorage
	    	
	    	// por defecto el navegador lo reconoce y no hace falta anteponer el 'window'
	    	localStorage
	    	
	    
	```
	
	Para limpiar/borrar datos:
	``` 
	    	window.localStorage.clear()
	    
	    
	```
	
	Setear un dato:
	``` 
	    	window.localStorage.setItem('item','value')
	    
	    
	```
	
	Obtener su valor:
	``` 
	    	window.localStorage.getItem('item')
	    	// value
	    	
	    
	```
	
	En [_**localStorage**_](https://developer.mozilla.org/es/docs/Web/API/Window/localStorage) no puedo guardar objetos directamente. Para poder hacerlo, hay que previamente convertir el objeto en un string.  
	Esto puedo hacerlo con el m√©todo, tambi√©n nativo de javascript, [_**JASON.stringify()**_](https://developer.mozilla.org/es/docs/Web/JavaScript/Referencia/Objetos_globales/JSON/stringify):
	``` 
	    	var object = JSON.stringify({'flor': 'roja'})
	    	window.localStorage.setItem('item', object)
	    	window.localStorage.getItem('item')
	    	// "{"flor":"roja"}"
	    
	    
	```
	
	Para re-convertirlo en objeto luego de obtenerlo puedo usar [_**JSON.parse**_](https://developer.mozilla.org/es/docs/Web/JavaScript/Referencia/Objetos_globales/JSON/parse):
	``` 
	    	const objectBack = window.localStorage.getItem('item')
	    	
	    	JSON.parse(objectBack)
	    	// {flor: "roja"}
	    	      flor: "roja"
	    	      > __proto__: Object
	    
	    
	```

* **Edgar Ramirez** (2)

	
	ejemplo de como guardar un objeto en el localstorage por medio de una key y luego imprimirlo por consola
	``` 
	    var testList = [
	       {
	           nombre: "CARLOS"
	       },
	       {
	           nombre: "GERONIMO"
	       },
	       {
	           nombre: "NICOLAS"
	       },
	       {
	           nombre: "LUCAS"
	       }
	    ]
	    
	    if(!localStorage.getItem("list")) {
	    
	       localStorage.setItem("list", JSON.stringify(testList))
	    }
	    
	    
	    functionnombre (key) {
	    
	       console.log(key)
	    
	    
	       if(localStorage.getItem(key)) {
	    
	              returnJSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key))
	           }
	    
	               else { return []
	    
	               }
	    
	    }
	    
	    console.log(nombre(prompt('Ingresa una key')))```
	    
	```

	* **Edward Steven Ramos Palacios** (1)

		
		localStorage es una API que guarda valores en **clave valor**.  
		Puedes guardar un objeto sin parsearlo a string primero pero, cuando lo consultes te va a devolver **[object] [object]**  
		por eso es necesario parsearlos a string para guardarlos y al recuperarlos los parseas a JSON de nuevo.

	    if(!localStorage.getItem("list")) {
	    
	       localStorage.setItem("list", JSON.stringify(testList))
	    }```
	    
	```

* **Sergio Minei** (15)

	
	Revisar si los datos se encuentran en cache.
	``` 
	    asyncfunctioncacheExist(category) {
	      const listName = `${category}List`;
	      const cacheList = window.localStorage.getItem(listName);
	    
	      if (cacheList)
	        returnJSON.parse(cacheList);
	      
	      const { data: { movies: data } } = await getData(`${BASE_API}list_movies.json?genre=${category}`);
	      window.localStorage.setItem(listName, JSON.stringify(data));
	      return data;
	    }
	    
	```
	
	Si se desea volver a traer los datos se puede hacer lo siguiente:
	
	  * Poner un bot√≥n que traiga los datos
	  * Hacer un setTimeout que borre el localStorage.
	
	
	
	Si quieren ver el resumen completo del curso lo pueden ver [aqu√≠](https://github.com/MineiToshio/CursosPlatzi/tree/master/Curso%20de%20jQuery%20a%20JavaScript). Lo ir√© actualizando a medida que vaya avanzando con el curso.

* **David Jim√©nez Mirayo** (6)

	
	Me gustar√≠a compartir esta peque√±a modificaci√≥n, que permite reutilizar la funci√≥n que renderiza las pel√≠culas, de forma que podemos incluir tantas categor√≠as como deseemos (siempre que incluyamos el c√≥digo con el ‚Äòid‚Äô correspondiente en el html). En mi caso, he a√±adido ‚Äòcomedy‚Äô y ‚Äòadventure‚Äô y funciona a la perfecci√≥n.
	
	Habr√≠a que incluir el siguiente c√≥gigo:
	``` 
	    const categories = ['action', 'drama', 'animation', 'comedy', 'adventure']
	      let lists = {}
	      asyncfunctionrenderCategoryList (category) {
	        constlist = await cacheExist(category)
	        lists[category] = list
	        const $container = document.querySelector(`#${category}`)
	        renderMovieList(list, $container, category)
	      }
	    
	      categories.forEach((category) => renderCategoryList(category))
	    
	```
	
	Este c√≥digo sustituir√≠a a esto:
	``` 
	      const actionList = await cacheExist('action')
	      const $actionContainer = document.querySelector('#action')
	      renderMovieList(actionList, $actionContainer, 'action')
	    
	      const dramaList = await cacheExist('drama')
	      const $dramaContainer = document.getElementById('drama')
	      renderMovieList(dramaList, $dramaContainer, 'drama')
	    
	      const animationList = await cacheExist('animation')
	      const $animationContainer = document.getElementById('animation')
	      renderMovieList(animationList, $animationContainer, 'animation')
	    
	```
	
	Finalmente, para que funcionen los modales, habr√≠a que cambiar la funci√≥n ‚ÄòfindMovie‚Äô, que quedar√≠a como sigue:
	``` 
	    functionfindMovie(id, category){
	        constlist = lists[category]
	        return findById(list, id)
	      }
	    
	```

	Complementando un poco lo que menciona Leonidas, Javascript nos permite utilizar otros tipos de datos como si fueran booleanos.
	
	‚ÄúEn JavaScript, un valor verdadero es un valor que se considera true/verdadero cuando es evaluado en un contexto Booleano. Todos los valores son verdaderos a menos que se definan como falso (es decir, excepto false, 0, ‚Äú‚Äù, null, undefined, y NaN).‚Äù‚Ä¶  
	[Truthy-MDN](https://developer.mozilla.org/es/docs/Glossary/Truthy)

* **abdielalvarez** (2)

	
	Mi aporte, c√≥digo 100% funcional con retos terminados, con cach√© para la lista de pel√≠culas de la nav bar y de los usuarios random, espero ser de ayuda para alguien que lo necesite üòÉ
	``` 
	    // GETTING DATA FROM LOCAL STORAGE
	    
	    (async function load() {
	    
	      async function getData(url) {
	        const response = await fetch(url);
	        const data = await response.json();
	        if (data.data.movie_count > 0) { 
	          return data;
	        }
	        throw new Error('No se encontr√≥ ningun resultado');
	      }
	      const $form = document.getElementById('form');
	      const $home = document.getElementById('home');
	      const $featuringContainer = document.getElementById('featuring');
	    
	      function setAttributes($element, attributes) {
	        for (const attribute in attributes) {
	          $element.setAttribute(attribute, attributes[attribute]);
	        }
	      }
	      const BASE_API = 'https://yts.lt/api/v2/';
	    
	      function featuringTemplate(peli) {
	        return (
	          `
	          <div class="featuring">
	            <div class="featuring-image">
	              <img src="${peli.medium_cover_image}" width="70" height="100" alt="">
	            </div>
	            <div class="featuring-content">
	              <p class="featuring-title">Pelicula encontrada</p>
	              <p class="featuring-album">${peli.title}</p>
	            </div>
	          </div>
	          `
	        )
	      }
	    
	      $form.addEventListener('submit', async (event) => {
	        event.preventDefault();
	        $home.classList.add('search-active')
	        const $loader = document.createElement('img');
	        setAttributes($loader, {
	          src: 'src/images/loader.gif',
	          height: 50,
	          width: 50,
	        })
	        $featuringContainer.append($loader);
	    
	        const data = new FormData($form);
	        try {
	          const {
	            data: {
	              movies: pelis
	            }
	          } = await getData(`${BASE_API}list_movies.json?limit=1&query_term=${data.get('name')}`)
	    
	          const HTMLString = featuringTemplate(pelis[0]);
	          $featuringContainer.innerHTML = HTMLString;
	        } catch(error) {
	          alert(error.message);
	          $loader.remove();
	          $home.classList.remove('search-active');
	        }
	      })
	    
	      // -----------comedy loader-----------------------------------------------------------------------
	    
	      const $img2 = document.createElement('img');
	      setAttributes($img2, {
	        src: 'src/images/loader.gif',
	        height: 50,
	        width: 50
	      })
	      const $comedyContainer = document.getElementById('comedyList')
	      $comedyContainer.append($img2)
	    
	      // -----------users loader-----------------------------------------------------------------------
	    
	      const $img3 = document.createElement('img');
	      setAttributes($img3, {
	        src: 'src/images/loader.gif',
	        height: 50,
	        width: 50,
	      })
	      const $usersContainer = document.getElementById('usersList');
	      $usersContainer.append($img3)
	    
	      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	    
	      function videoItemTemplate(movie, category) {
	        return (
	          `<div class="primaryPlaylistItem" data-id="${movie.id}" data-category=${category}>
	            <div class="primaryPlaylistItem-image">
	              <img src="${movie.medium_cover_image}">
	            </div>
	            <h4 class="primaryPlaylistItem-title">
	              ${movie.title}
	            </h4>
	          </div>`
	        )
	      }
	      function createTemplate(HTMLString) {
	        const html = document.implementation.createHTMLDocument();
	        html.body.innerHTML = HTMLString;
	        return html.body.children[0];
	      }
	      function addEventClick($element) {
	        $element.addEventListener('click', () => {
	          showModal($element)
	        })
	      }
	      function renderMovieList(list, $container, category) {
	        $container.children[0].remove();
	        list.forEach((movie) => {
	          const HTMLString = videoItemTemplate(movie, category);
	          const movieElement = createTemplate(HTMLString);
	          $container.append(movieElement);
	          const image = movieElement.querySelector('img');
	          image.addEventListener('load', (event) => {
	            event.srcElement.classList.add('fadeIn');
	          })
	          addEventClick(movieElement);
	        })
	      }
	    
	      async function cacheExist (category) {
	        const listName = `${category}List`
	        const cacheList = localStorage.getItem(listName)
	        if(cacheList) {
	          return JSON.parse(cacheList)
	        }
	        const { data: { movies: data } } = await getData(`${BASE_API}list_movies.json?genre=${category}`)
	        localStorage.setItem(listName, JSON.stringify(data))
	        return data
	      }
	    
	      const actionList = await cacheExist('action')
	      const $actionContainer = document.querySelector('#action');
	      renderMovieList(actionList, $actionContainer, 'action');
	    
	      const dramaList = await cacheExist('drama')
	      const $dramaContainer = document.getElementById('drama');
	      renderMovieList(dramaList, $dramaContainer, 'drama');
	    
	      const animationList = await cacheExist('animation')
	      const $animationContainer = document.getElementById('animation');
	      renderMovieList(animationList, $animationContainer, 'animation');
	    
	      const $modal = document.getElementById('modal');
	      const $overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
	      const $hideModal = document.getElementById('hide-modal');
	    
	      const $modalTitle = $modal.querySelector('h1');
	      const $modalImage = $modal.querySelector('img');
	      const $modalDescription = $modal.querySelector('p');
	    
	      function findById(list, id) {
	        return list.find(movie => movie.id === parseInt(id, 10))
	      }
	    
	      function findMovie(id, category) {
	        switch (category) {
	          case 'action' : {
	            return findById(actionList, id)
	          }
	          case 'drama' : {
	            return findById(dramaList, id)
	          }
	          default: {
	            return findById(animationList, id)
	          }
	        }
	      }
	    
	      function showModal($element) {
	        $overlay.classList.add('active');
	        $modal.style.animation = 'modalIn .8s forwards';
	        const id = $element.dataset.id;
	        const category = $element.dataset.category;
	        const data = findMovie(id, category);
	    
	        $modalTitle.textContent = data.title;
	        $modalImage.setAttribute('src', data.medium_cover_image);
	        $modalDescription.textContent = data.description_full
	      }
	    
	      $hideModal.addEventListener('click', hideModal);
	      function hideModal() {
	        $overlay.classList.remove('active');
	        $modal.style.animation = 'modalOut .8s forwards';
	      }
	    
	      // ---------Comedy list exercise for playlist item----------
	    
	      const comedyList = await cacheExist('comedy')
	    
	      function myPlaylistItemTemplate (movie) {
	        return (
	          `<li class="myPlaylist-item">
	            <a href="#">
	              <span>
	                ${movie.title}
	              </span>
	            </a>
	          </li>`
	        )
	      }
	    
	      try {
	        $comedyContainer.children[0].remove();
	        comedyList.forEach(movie => {
	          const HTMLString = myPlaylistItemTemplate(movie)
	          const html = document.implementation.createHTMLDocument()
	          html.body.innerHTML = HTMLString
	          $comedyContainer.append(html.body.children[0])
	          $comedyContainer.classList.add('fadeIn');
	        }) 
	      } catch (error) {
	        throw new Error('Lista de comedia no fue resuelta')
	      }
	      
	    
	      // ----------User random generator exercise for profiles-----------
	    
	      async function cacheUsersExist () {
	        const listName = 'userList'
	        const cacheList = localStorage.getItem(listName)
	        if(cacheList) {
	          return JSON.parse(cacheList)
	        }
	        const { results: usersList } = await getUsers('https://randomuser.me/api/?results=20')
	        localStorage.setItem(listName, JSON.stringify(usersList))
	        return usersList
	      }
	    
	      const usersList = await cacheUsersExist()
	      
	      async function getUsers(url) {
	        const response = await fetch(url);
	        const data = await response.json();
	        return data
	      }
	      
	      function playlistFriendsItemTemplate({ name: { first }, picture: { thumbnail } }) {
	        return (
	          `<li class="playlistFriends-item">
	            <a href="#">
	              <img src="${thumbnail}" alt="${first}" />
	              <span>
	                ${first}
	              </span>
	            </a>
	          </li>`
	        )
	      }
	    
	      try {
	        $usersContainer.children[0].remove();
	        usersList.forEach(user => {    
	          const HTMLString = playlistFriendsItemTemplate(user)
	          const html = document.implementation.createHTMLDocument()
	          html.body.innerHTML = HTMLString
	          $usersContainer.append(html.body.children[0])
	          $usersContainer.classList.add('fadeIn');
	        })
	      } catch (error) {
	        throw new Error('No se pudieron encontrar usuarios')
	      }
	    
	    })()
	    
	```

	    asyncfunctioncacheExist(genre) {
	        const cacheList = window.localStorage.getItem(`${genre}List`)
	        if(cacheList) {
	          setTimeout(async () => {
	            window.localStorage.removeItem(`${genre}List`);
	            const {data: {movies}} = await getMovies(`${BASE_MOVIES_API}list_movies.json?genre=${genre}`)
	            window.localStorage.setItem(`${genre}List`, JSON.stringify(movies))
	          }, 1000)

	        } else {
	          const {data: {movies}} = await getMovies(`${BASE_MOVIES_API}list_movies.json?genre=${genre}`)

	        }
	      }

* **Aaron Felipe Isaacs** (1)

	
	Buen d√°i,
	
	Documentaci√≥n del curso en markdown en mi repositorio
	
	Web page: [](https://github.com/afisaacs/jquerytojavascript)  
	Repository: [](https://github.com/afisaacs/jquerytojavascript)
	``` 
	    const load = async () => {
	      const API_MOVIE = 'https://yts.lt/api/v2/list_movies.json'
	      const API_USER = 'https://randomuser.me/api/'
	      const movies = ['action', 'drama', 'animation']
	      const listMovies = {}
	    
	      const $form = document.getElementById('form')
	      const $home = document.getElementById('home')
	      const $featuringContainer = document.getElementById('featuring')
	    
	      const $overlay = document.getElementById('overlay')
	      const $modal = document.getElementById('modal')
	      const $hideModal = document.getElementById('hide-modal')
	    
	      const $modalTitle = document.getElementById('modal-title')
	      const $modalImage = document.querySelector('.modal-content img')
	      const $modalDescription = document.querySelector('.modal-content p')
	    
	      const getDataMovies = async (url, filters) => getData(url, filters, 'movie')
	    
	      const getData = async (url, filters, type) => {
	        let paramGet = ''
	        if (filters) {
	          paramGet += '?'
	          Object.keys(filters).forEach(filter => {
	            if (paramGet.length > 1) {
	              paramGet += '&'
	            }
	            paramGet += `${filter}=${filters[filter]}`
	          })
	        }
	        const action = await fetch(`${url}${paramGet}`)
	        const data = await action.json()
	        if (type === 'movie') {
	          if (data.data.movie_count > 0) {
	            return data
	          } else {
	            throw ('The movie was not found')
	          }
	        }
	        return data
	      }
	    
	      const videoItemTemplate = ({ medium_cover_image, title, id }, category) => {
	        return (
	        `<div class="primaryPlaylistItem" data-id="${id}" data-category="${category}">
	          <div class="primaryPlaylistItem-image">
	            <img style="opacity: 0;" src="${medium_cover_image}">
	          </div>
	          <h4 class="primaryPlaylistItem-title">
	            ${title}
	          </h4>
	        </div>`
	        )
	      }
	    
	      const featuringTemplate = ({ medium_cover_image, title }) => {
	        return (
	          `<div class="featuring">
	            <div class="featuring-image">
	              <img src="${medium_cover_image}" width="70" height="100" alt="">
	            </div>
	            <div class="featuring-content">
	              <p class="featuring-title">Pelicula encontrada</p>
	              <p class="featuring-album">${title}</p>
	            </div>
	          </div>`
	        )
	      }
	    
	      const userTemplate = ({ picture: {medium: image}, name}) => {
	        return (
	          `<li class="playlistFriends-item">
	            <a href="#">
	              <img src="${image}" />
	              <span style="text-transform: capitalize;">
	                ${name.title} ${name.first} ${name.last} 
	              </span>
	            </a>
	          </li>`
	        )
	      }
	    
	      const playListTemplate = ({ title }) => {
	        return (
	          `<li class="myPlaylist-item">
	            <a href="#">
	              <span>
	                ${title}
	              </span>
	            </a>
	          </li>`
	        )
	      }
	    
	      const findMovie = (id, category) => listMovies[category].find(item => item.id === parseInt(id, 10))
	      
	      const showModal = ({ currentTarget: $element }) => {
	        $overlay.classList.add('active')
	        $modal.style.animation = 'modalIn .8s forwards'
	        const { id, category } = $element.dataset
	        const data = findMovie(id, category)
	    
	        $modalTitle.textContent = data.title
	        $modalImage.setAttribute('src', data.medium_cover_image)
	        $modalDescription.textContent = data.description_full
	      }
	    
	      const addHideModalListener = () => {
	        $hideModal.addEventListener('click', () => {
	          setTimeout(() => $overlay.classList.remove('active'), 800)
	          $modal.style.animation = 'modalOut .8s forwards'
	        })
	      }
	    
	      const addAttributes = (element, attributes) => {
	        Object.keys(attributes).forEach(attr => element.setAttribute(attr, attributes[attr]))
	      }
	    
	      const addSubmitListener = () => {
	        $form.addEventListener('submit', async event => {
	          $featuringContainer.innerHTML = ""
	          event.preventDefault()
	          $home.classList.add('search-active')
	          const $loader = document.createElement('img')
	          addAttributes($loader, {
	            src: './src/images/loader.gif',
	            height: '50px',
	            width: '50px'
	          })
	          $featuringContainer.appendChild($loader)
	    
	          const data = new FormData($form)
	          const searchInput = data.get('name')
	          try {
	            const { data: { movies } } = await getDataMovies(API_MOVIE, {query_term: searchInput})
	            const htmlString = featuringTemplate(movies[0])
	            $featuringContainer.innerHTML = htmlString
	          } catch (error) {
	            alert(error)
	            $featuringContainer.removeChild($loader)
	            $home.classList.remove('search-active')
	          }
	        })
	      }
	    
	      const putMovieComponent = (lstMovies, element, genre) => {
	        element.innerHTML = ""
	        lstMovies.forEach(movie => {
	          const htmlString = videoItemTemplate(movie, genre)
	          const html = document.implementation.createHTMLDocument()
	          html.body.innerHTML = htmlString
	          const component = html.body.children[0]
	          component.addEventListener('click', event => showModal(event))
	          const image = component.querySelector('img')
	          image.addEventListener('load', event => event.srcElement.classList.add('fadeIn'))
	          element.appendChild(component)
	        })
	      }
	    
	      const putUserComponent = (lstUser, element) => {
	        element.innerHTML = ""
	        lstUser.forEach(user => {
	          const htmlString = userTemplate(user)
	          const html = document.implementation.createHTMLDocument()
	          html.body.innerHTML = htmlString
	          const component = html.body.children[0]
	          element.appendChild(component)
	        })
	      }
	      
	      const putPlaylistComponent = (lstMovies, element) => {
	        element.innerHTML = ""
	        lstMovies.forEach((movie) => {
	          const htmlString = playListTemplate(movie)
	          const html = document.implementation.createHTMLDocument()
	          html.body.innerHTML = htmlString
	          const component = html.body.children[0]
	          element.appendChild(component)
	        })
	      }
	    
	      const renderMovies = async genre => {
	        let apidata
	        if (!window.localStorage.getItem(genre)) {
	          apidata = await getDataMovies(API_MOVIE, {genre})
	          window.localStorage.setItem(genre, JSON.stringify(apidata))
	        } else {
	          apidata = JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem(genre))
	        }
	        const $container = document.getElementById(genre)
	        putMovieComponent(apidata.data.movies, $container, genre)
	        listMovies[genre] = apidata.data.movies
	      }
	      
	      const renderUsers = async () => {
	        const apidata = await getData(API_USER, {results: 10})
	        const $container = document.getElementById('lst-friends')
	        putUserComponent(apidata.results, $container)
	      }
	      
	      const renderPlayList = async () => {
	        const apidata = await getDataMovies(API_MOVIE, {limit: 10})
	        const $container = document.getElementById('playlist')
	        putPlaylistComponent(apidata.data.movies, $container)
	      }
	    
	      addSubmitListener()
	      addHideModalListener()
	      movies.forEach(movie => renderMovies(movie))
	      renderUsers()
	      renderPlayList()
	    }
	    
	    load()
	    
	    
	```

* **heysoypaez** (1)

	
	¬øPor qu√© es necesario colocar el await en este c√≥digo?
	``` 
	    		const animationList = await cacheExist("animation")
	    
	```
	
	Si hay una sola funci√≥n seg√∫n comprendo javascript la deberia ejecutar inmediatamente, y m√°s tomando en cuenta que el c√≥digo dentro de esa funci√≥n tiene async await para la informaci√≥n que necesita
	
	Si es una funci√≥n llamando otra funci√≥n alli si empieza a jugar su papel el asincronismo
	
	Si alguien me pudiera ilustrar un poco con ejemplos y su experiencia me ayudaria un mont√≥n

	* **Eduardo Hidalgo D√≠az Rugama** (7)

		
		async y await es para que hagas cosas paralelamente. No es tema de ‚Äúsolo tengo una linea de c√≥digo‚Äù.
		
		Si por ejemplo, yo hago una sola petici√≥n a una api con fetch sin async/wait, pero usando React, durante los 5 segundos que se demore el fetch la aplicaci√≥n va a estar freezeada, y el usuario no podr√° usar nada de la app. S√∫male la p√©sima experiencia de usuario de que la app est√© freezeada.
		
		Tambi√©n te sirve (usando promesas) para ejecutar animaciones como loaders para demostrarle al usuario que debe esperar por el contenido. Mientras est√° recibiendo la data, tu le dices con un loader ‚Äúesperame‚Äù.

* **Carlos Jes√∫s Fern√°ndez Salazar** (1)

	
	Creo que pude redundar un poco menos pero este es mi c√≥digo de **cacheExists** :
	``` 
	    asyncfunctioncacheExists(item) {
	        if (item == 'friends') {
	          cacheList = window.localStorage.getItem(item);
	          if (cacheList) {
	            returnJSON.parse(cacheList);
	          } else {
	            const { results: friends } = await getData(`${USER_API}${USER_QTY}`);
	            window.localStorage.setItem(friends, JSON.stringify(friends));
	            return friends;
	          }
	        } elseif (item == 'likedList'){
	          cacheList = window.localStorage.getItem(item);
	          if (cacheList) {
	            returnJSON.parse(cacheList);
	          } else {
	            const { data: { movies: likedList }} = await getData(`${MOVIES_API}${MOVIES_SORT}download_count${MOVIES_QTY}10`);
	            window.localStorage.setItem(likedList, JSON.stringify(likedList));
	            return likedList;
	          }
	        } else {
	          const listName = `${item}List`
	          const cacheList = window.localStorage.getItem(listName);
	          if (cacheList) {
	            returnJSON.parse(cacheList);
	          } else {
	            const { data: { movies: data }} = await getData(`${MOVIES_API}${MOVIES_GENRE}${item}`);
	            window.localStorage.setItem(listName, JSON.stringify(data));
	            return data;
	          }
	        }
	      }
	    
	```

	* **Erik Ochoa (Platzi)** (1)

* **Jos√© Bryan Aranda Figueroa** (1)

	* **Edward Steven Ramos Palacios** (1)

		
		Una funci√≥n `async` siempre debe retornar una promesa. Cuando retornas `return JSON.parse(cacheList);` estas retornando un objeto, pero no una promesa resuelta con la data.
		
		Lo que puedes hacer es refactorizar, y extraer en una funci√≥n nueva lo que tiene que ver con validar y retornar la data desde el local storage.

* **Luis Felipe Andr√©s Barraza Vega** (4)

	
	Hola amigos les dejo mi archivo JS donde aplique el reto y puse a la izquierda un playlist de peliculas y abajo usuarios con su avatar, con la api randomuser todo hecho con vanillaJS porsupuesto:
	``` 
	    (async function load(){
	    
	        async function getUser(url) {
	          const response = await fetch(url);
	          const data = await response.json();
	            users= data;
	        }
	        getUser('https://randomuser.me/api/?inc=name,picture&results=10')
	        //const listUserC = users.results.length;
	    
	    
	        //await
	        async function getData(url) {
	          const response = await fetch(url);
	          const data = await response.json();
	          if (data.data.movie_count > 0) {
	            // aqu√≠ se acaba
	            return data;
	          }
	          // si no hay pelis aqu√≠ continua
	          throw new Error('No se encontr√≥ ningun resultado');
	        }
	    
	        const $form = document.getElementById('form');
	        const $home = document.getElementById('home');
	        const $featuringContainer = document.getElementById('featuring');
	    
	        function setAttributes($element, attributes){
	          for (const attribute in attributes) {
	            $element.setAttribute(attribute, attributes[attribute])
	          }
	    
	    
	        }
	    
	        const BASE_API = 'https://yts.am/api/v2/'
	        const BASE_USER = 'https://randomuser.me/api'
	    
	    
	    
	        function featuringTemplate(peli){
	          return(
	            `<div class="featuring">
	              <div class="featuring-image">
	                <img src="${peli.medium_cover_image}" width="70" height="100" alt="">
	              </div>
	              <div class="featuring-content">
	                <p class="featuring-title">Pelicula encontrada</p>
	                <p class="featuring-album">${peli.title}</p>
	              </div>
	            </div>`
	          )
	        }
	    
	        $form.addEventListener('submit', async (event)=>{
	          event.preventDefault();
	          $home.classList.add('search-active')
	          const $loader = document.createElement('img');
	          setAttributes($loader,{
	            src:'src/images/loader.gif',
	            height: 50,
	            width: 50,
	          })
	          $featuringContainer.append($loader);
	    
	          const data = new FormData($form);
	          //destructuracion de objetos
	          try {
	            const {
	              data: {
	                movies: pelis
	              }
	            } = await getData(`${BASE_API}list_movies.json?limit=1&query_term=${data.get('name')}`)
	            const HTMLString = featuringTemplate(pelis[0])
	            $featuringContainer.innerHTML = HTMLString;
	          } catch(error){
	            alert('Pelicula no encontrada');
	            $loader.remove();
	            $home.classList.remove('search-active');
	          }
	    
	    
	        })
	    
	    
	    
	        function videoItemTemplate(movie, category){
	          return (
	            //templateLiterals:
	            //${} permite integrar variables a html para hacer un html dinamico
	              `<div class="primaryPlaylistItem" data-id="${movie.id}" data-category=${category}>
	                <div class="primaryPlaylistItem-image">
	                  <img src="${movie.medium_cover_image}">
	                </div>
	                <h4 class="primaryPlaylistItem-title">
	                  ${movie.title}
	                </h4>
	              </div>`
	            )
	        }
	    
	        function playListTemplate(movie){
	          return(
	          `
	          <ol class="myPlaylist">
	            <la class="myPlaylist-item">
	              <a href="#">
	                <span>
	                  ${movie.title} - ${movie.genres[0]}
	                </span>
	              </a>
	            </la>
	          </ol>
	    
	          `)
	        }
	    
	    
	        //console.log(videoItemTemplate('src/images/covers/bitcoin.jpg', 'bitcoin'))
	    
	    
	    
	        function createTemplate(HTMLString){
	          const html = document.implementation.createHTMLDocument();
	          html.body.innerHTML = HTMLString;
	          return html.body.children[0];
	        }
	    
	        function addEventClick($element){
	          $element.addEventListener('click',()=>{
	            //alert('click')
	            showModal($element)
	          })
	        }
	    
	        function renderUser(list,$container){
	          $container.children[0].remove();
	    
	          for (var i = 0; i < list; i++) {
	            const HTMLString = `
	    
	            <ul class="playlistFriends">
	              <li class="playlistFriends-item">
	                <a href="#">
	                  <img src="${users.results[i].picture.thumbnail}" />
	                  <span>
	                    ${users.results[i].name.last}, ${users.results[i].name.first}
	                  </span>
	                </a>
	              </li>
	    
	    
	    
	            </ul>
	    
	              `;
	            const userElement = createTemplate(HTMLString);
	            $container.append(userElement)
	          }
	    
	    
	    
	    
	        }
	    
	      
	    
	        function renderPlayList(list, $container, category){
	          $container.children[0].remove();
	          list.forEach((movie) => {
	            const HTMLString = playListTemplate(movie, category);
	            const movieElement = createTemplate(HTMLString)
	            $container.append(movieElement);
	    
	    
	          })
	        }
	    
	        function renderMovieList(list, $container, category){
	          $container.children[0].remove();
	          list.forEach((movie) => {
	    
	            const HTMLString = videoItemTemplate(movie, category);
	            const movieElement = createTemplate(HTMLString)
	            $container.append(movieElement);
	            const image = movieElement.querySelector('img');
	            image.addEventListener('load', () => {
	              event.srcElement.classList.add('fadeIn');
	            })
	            addEventClick(movieElement);
	    
	          })
	        }
	    
	    
	    
	    
	    
	        async function cacheExist(category){
	          const listName = `${category}List`;
	          const cacheList = window.localStorage.getItem(listName);
	    
	          if(cacheList){
	            return JSON.parse(cacheList);
	          }
	          const {data: {movies:data}} = await getData(`${BASE_API}list_movies.json?genre=${category}`)
	          //const { "results":user} = await getUser('https://randomuser.me/api/?inc=name')
	    
	          window.localStorage.setItem('listName', JSON.stringify(data))
	          return data;
	        }
	    
	    
	    
	    
	    
	    
	    
	        //const {data: {movies:actionList}} = await getData(`${BASE_API}list_movies.json?genre=action`)
	        const actionList = await cacheExist('action');
	        //window.localStorage.setItem('actionList', JSON.stringify(actionList))
	        const $actionContainer = document.querySelector('#action');
	        renderMovieList(actionList,$actionContainer, 'action')
	    
	        //const {data: {movies:dramaList}} = await getData(`${BASE_API}list_movies.json?genre=drama`)
	        //window.localStorage.setItem('dramaList', JSON.stringify(dramaList))
	        const dramaList = await cacheExist('drama');
	        const $dramaContainer = document.querySelector('#drama');
	        renderMovieList(dramaList,$dramaContainer, 'drama')
	    
	        // const {data: {movies:animationList}} = await getData(`${BASE_API}list_movies.json?genre=animation`)
	        // window.localStorage.setItem('animationList', JSON.stringify(animationList))
	        const animationList = await cacheExist('animation');
	        const $animationContainer = document.querySelector('#animation');
	        renderMovieList(animationList,$animationContainer, 'animation')
	    
	        const nameMovie = await cacheExist('');
	        const $nameMovie = document.querySelector('#playlist');
	        renderPlayList(nameMovie,$nameMovie);
	    
	        //const pickUser = getUser('https://randomuser.me/api/?inc=name,picture')
	        const $userContainer = document.querySelector('#users');
	        const listPerson = users.results.length;
	        renderUser(listPerson,$userContainer)
	    
	    
	    
	    
	    
	    
	    
	        // selector => .home
	        //solucion de seleccion de selectores con jquery
	        //const $home = $('.home .list #item');
	        //solucion de selectores en vanillaJS
	        const $modal = document.getElementById('modal');
	        const $overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
	        const $hideModal = document.getElementById('hide-modal');
	    
	        //buscar dentro de clases
	        const $modalImage = $modal.querySelector('img');
	        const $modalTitle = $modal.querySelector('h1');
	        const $modalDescription = $modal.querySelector('p');
	    
	        function findById(list, id){
	          return list.find(movie => movie.id === parseInt(id,10))
	        }
	        function findMovie(id, category){
	          switch (category) {
	            case 'action':{
	              return findById(actionList,id)
	            }
	            case 'drama':{
	              return findById(dramaList,id)
	            }
	            default: {
	              return findById(animationList,id)
	            }
	          }
	        }
	    
	        function showModal($element){
	          $overlay.classList.add('active');
	          $modal.style.animation = 'modalIn .8s forwards';
	          const id = $element.dataset.id;
	          const category = $element.dataset.category;
	          const data = findMovie(id,category)
	    
	          $modalImage.setAttribute('src',data.medium_cover_image);
	          $modalTitle.textContent=data.title;
	          $modalDescription.textContent = data.description_full;
	        }
	    
	        $hideModal.addEventListener('click', hideModal);
	        function hideModal(){
	          $overlay.classList.remove('active');
	          $modal.style.animation = 'modalOut .8s forwards';
	        }
	    
	    
	    
	    
	    
	      })()//sugarSintax para autoejecutar funcion
	    
	```

	    (async function load() {
	      const $modal = document.getElementById('modal');
	      const $hideModal = document.getElementById('hide-modal');
	      const $seeker= document.getElementsByTagName('input');
	      const $seekerContent= $seeker.value;

	      const $modalImage = $modal.querySelector('img');
	      const $modalDescription = $modal.querySelector('p');
	      const $actionContainer = document.querySelector('#action');
	      const $dramaContainer = document.querySelector('#drama');
	      const $animationContainer = document.querySelector('#animation');
	      const $result=document.querySelector('.search-active')
	    
	      const $featuringContainer = document.querySelector('#featuring');
	      const $form = document.getElementById('form');
	      const $overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');

	      function setAttributes($element, attributes){
	        for (const attribute in attributes) {
	          $element.setAttribute(attribute, attributes[attribute])
	        }
	      }
	    
	      async function getData(url) {
	          const response = await fetch(url);
	          jsonRseponse= response.json()
	          return jsonRseponse
	          //ANCHOR funci√≥n para traer las pelis
	      }
	    
	      const displaySeekingResult=async()=>{
	        event.preventDefault()
	        $home.classList.add('search-active')
	        //ANCHOR aqu√≠ mostramos la barrita que nos sale al buscar una peli
	        
	        const $loader=document.createElement('img')
	        //NOTE $loader.setAttribute('src', 'loader.gif')
	        setAttributes($loader,{
	          src:'src/images/loader.gif',
	          height: 50,
	          width: 50
	        })
	        $featuringContainer.append($loader)
	        function featuringTemplate(peli){
	          return(
	            `<div class="featuring">
	              <div class="featuring-image">
	                <img src="${peli.medium_cover_image}" width="70" height="100" alt="pel√≠cula encontrada">
	              </div>
	              <div class="featuring-content">
	                <p class="featuring-title">Pelicula encontrada</p>
	                <p class="featuring-album">${peli.title}</p>
	              </div>
	            </div>`)
	        }
	    
	        const data= new FormData($form)
	        const findMovie= (list, data)=>{
	          const action =({category})=> category == 'action'
	          //ese category en realidad viene dentro de un
	          //parametro que se le pasa en el .filter que es el mismo
	          //objeto al que le ponemos esa propiedad
	          const drama =({category})=> category == 'drama'
	          const animation =({category})=> category == 'animation'
	          /*NOTE aqu√≠ hay que poner OBLIGATORIAMENTE el parametro, lo que le 
	          estamos diciendo es que vea dentro de todos los list 
	          y que revise el list.category, si no lo ponemos solo va a 
	          revisar por encima
	          */ 
	          
	        const actionMovieList= list.filter(action)
	        console.log(actionMovieList)
	        const dramaMovieList= list.filter(drama)
	        const animationMovieList= list.filter(animation)
	    
	    
	    
	          const movieFound = ()=>list.find(arr => arr.id === parseInt(data));
	          return movieFound
	        }
	        findMovie(generalMovieList, data.get('name'))
	        const peli= getData(`https://yts.mx/api/v2/list_movies.json?limit=1&query_term=${data.get('name')}`)
	        //NOTE limit=1 es una propiedad del m√©todo GET, que nos da un l√≠mite del primerisimo resultado
	        //NOTE el query_term es de la api para traernos una pelicula en especifico
	        //NOTE El '&' entre los mencionados anteriormente es para denotar que son propiedades distintas
	        .then((data)=>{
	          $HTMLMovieFoundString=featuringTemplate(data.data.movies[0])
	          /**ANCHOR
	          esto por si solo nos retorna el objeto de html con los valores pero 
	          no los pone donde va, de eso de encarga el inner.HTML*/
	          $featuringContainer.innerHTML= $HTMLMovieFoundString
	          featuringTemplate(data)
	          return data
	        })
	        .catch((err)=>{
	          function featuringTemplateDefault(){
	            return(
	              `<div class="featuring">
	                <div class="featuring-image">
	                  <img src="https://www.evisionstore.com/images/notfound.png" width="70" height="100" alt="pel√≠cula encontrada">
	                </div>
	                <div class="featuring-content">
	                  <p class="featuring-title">Pelicula encontrada</p>
	                  <p class="featuring-album">movie '${data.get('name')}'not found :(</p>
	                </div>
	              </div>`)
	          }
	          $HTMLMovieFoundString= featuringTemplateDefault()
	            
	          $featuringContainer.innerHTML= $HTMLMovieFoundString
	    
	    
	        })
	      }
	    
	      $form.addEventListener('submit', displaySeekingResult);
	    
	    
	    
	      function videoItemTemplate(movie, category) {
	        return (
	          `<div class="primaryPlaylistItem" data-id="${movie.id}" data-category=${category}>
	            <div class="primaryPlaylistItem-image">
	              <img src="${movie.medium_cover_image}">
	            </div>
	            <h4 class="primaryPlaylistItem-title">
	              ${movie.title}
	            </h4>
	          </div>`
	        )
	      }

	      function createTemplate(htmlTags){
	          const html = document.implementation.createHTMLDocument();
	          html.body.innerHTML = htmlTags;
	          return html.body.children[0]
	      }
	    
	      function addEventClick($movieElement, movie){
	        const displayOverlay=()=>{
	          $overlay.classList.add('active')
	          //ANCHOR modal es la ventanita que nos sale al hacer click en las pelis
	          $modal.children[0].innerHTML= movie.title
	          $modalDescription.innerHTML= movie.description_full
	    
	          $modalImage.setAttribute('src', `${movie.medium_cover_image}`)
	          $modal.style.animation= 'modalIn .8s forwards'
	    
	          const hideOverlay=()=>{
	            $overlay.classList.remove('active')
	            $modal.style.animation= 'modalOut .8s forwards'
	          }
	    
	          $hideModal.addEventListener('click', hideOverlay)
	        }
	    
	    
	        const id = $movieElement.dataset.id
	        const category= $movieElement.dataset.category
	        $movieElement.addEventListener('click', displayOverlay)
	      }
	    
	    
	      
	      function renderMovies(list, $movieGenreContainer, category){
	    
	        $movieGenreContainer.children[0].remove()
	        
	        list.forEach((movie) => {
	          const id_Category= {
	            id: movie.id,
	            category: category
	          }
	          generalMovieList.push(id_Category)
	    
	          const HTMLString = videoItemTemplate(movie, category);
	          const html = createTemplate(HTMLString)
	          html.style.animation= 'fadeIn 2s forwards'
	          //NOTE aqu√≠ le decimos que nos ponga una animacion que ya estaba en 
	          //el styles.css que es fadeIn
	          $movieGenreContainer.append(html);
	          addEventClick(html, movie)
	          //ANCHOR esto adem√°s del dlcik pone el t√≠tulo del modal
	        })
	        
	      }
	      if(window.localStorage.dramaList===undefined && window.localStorage.actionList===undefined && window.localStorage.animationList===undefined)
	      //NOTE le decimos que si el localstorage de eso existe lo use, tiene que ser undefined para no, no puede ser false
	      {
	        const actionList= getData('https://yts.mx/api/v2/list_movies.json?genre=action')
	        .then(({data})=>{
	          renderMovies(data.movies, $actionContainer, 'action')
	          window.localStorage.setItem('actionList', JSON.stringify(data))
	        })
	        .then(()=>{
	          const dramaList= getData('https://yts.mx/api/v2/list_movies.json?genre=drama') 
	          return dramaList
	        })
	        .then(({data})=>{
	          renderMovies(data.movies, $dramaContainer, 'drama')
	          window.localStorage.setItem('dramaList',  JSON.stringify(data))
	        })
	        .then(()=>{
	          const animationList= getData('https://yts.mx/api/v2/list_movies.json?genre=animation') 
	          return animationList
	        })
	      //  window.localStorage.setItem('animationList', animationList)
	        .then(({data})=>{
	          renderMovies(data.movies, $animationContainer, 'animation')
	          window.localStorage.setItem('animationList',  JSON.stringify(data))
	        }).catch((err)=>console.log(err))
	      }
	    
	      else{
	        const cacheActionList=JSON.parse(window.localStorage.actionList)
	        const cacheDramaList=JSON.parse(window.localStorage.dramaList)
	        const cacheAnimationList=JSON.parse(window.localStorage.animationList)
	        //NOTE si no lo guardamos en una variable no funciona
	        renderMovies(cacheActionList.movies, $actionContainer, 'action')
	        renderMovies(cacheDramaList.movies, $dramaContainer, 'drama')
	        renderMovies(cacheAnimationList.movies, $animationContainer, 'animation')
	        console.log(ewe)
	        alert('asumaidre')
	      }
	    })()

* **David Daniel Castillo Nava** (0)

	
	 **As√≠ quedo mi c√≥digo!!**
	``` 
	    const API_BASE = 'https://yts.am/api/v2';
	    
	    (async function load(){
	    
	    	/*
	    	** Initial Variables
	    	*/
	    	const $home = document.getElementById('home');
	    	const $form = document.getElementById('form');
	    	const $featuringContainer = document.getElementById('featuring');
	    
	    	const $actionContainer = document.querySelector('#action');
	    	const $dramaContainer = document.getElementById('drama');
	    	const $animationContainer = document.getElementById('animation');
	    
	    	const $modal = document.getElementById('modal');
	    	const $overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
	    
	    	const $hideModal = document.getElementById('hide-modal');
	    	
	    	const $modalTitle = $modal.querySelector('h1');
	    	const $modalImage = $modal.querySelector('img');
	    	const $modalDescription = $modal.querySelector('p')
	    
	    	/*
	    	** Initial Fetch
	    	*/
	    
	    	async function cacheVerify(category) {
	    		const listName = `${category}List`;
	    		const cacheList = window.localStorage.getItem(listName);
	    
	    		if (cacheList) return JSON.stringify(cacheList)
	    
	    		const { data: {movies: data }} = await getData(`${API_BASE}/list_movies.json?genre=${category}`)
	    		window.localStorage.setItem(listName, JSON.stringify(data))
	    		return data
	    	}
	    
	    	// let [ reqAction, reqDrama, reqAnimation ] = await Promise.all([
	    	// 	fetch(`${API_BASE}/list_movies.json?genre=action`),
	    	// 	fetch(`${API_BASE}/list_movies.json?genre=drama`),
	    	// 	fetch(`${API_BASE}/list_movies.json?genre=animation`)
	    	// ])
	    
	    	
	    	const actionList = await cacheVerify('action')
	    	// window.localStorage.setItem('actionList', JSON.stringify(actionList))
	    	renderList(actionList, $actionContainer, 'listPlayer',{click:true, render: 'append', fadeIn: true}, 'action')
	    	const dramaList =await cacheVerify('drama')
	    	// window.localStorage.setItem('dramaList', JSON.stringify(dramaList))
	    	renderList(dramaList, $dramaContainer, 'listPlayer',{click:true, render: 'append', fadeIn: true}, 'drama')
	    	const animationList = await cacheVerify('animation')
	    	// window.localStorage.setItem('animationList', JSON.stringify(animationList))
	    	renderList(animationList, $animationContainer, 'listPlayer',{click:true, render: 'append', fadeIn: true}, 'animation')
	    
	    	
	    	/*
	    	** Functions
	    	*/
	    	async function getData(url) {
	    		const response = await fetch(url);
	    		
	    		const data = await response.json()
	    		if(data.data.movie_count > 0){
	    			return data;
	    		}
	    		
	    	}
	    
	    	function setAttributes($element, attributes) {
	    		for (const attribute in attributes) {
	    			$element.setAttribute(attribute, attributes[attribute])
	    		}
	    	}
	    
	    	function templateContent (template, content) {
	    		let hmtlContent;
	    		switch(template) {
	    			case 'listPlayer':
	    				hmtlContent = `
	    					<div data-id="${content.id}" data-category="${content.category}" class="primaryPlaylistItem">
	    						<div class="primaryPlaylistItem-image">
	    							<img src="${content.medium_cover_image}">
	    						</div>
	    						<h4 class="primaryPlaylistItem-title">
	    							${content.title_long}
	    						</h4>
	    					</div>
	    				`
	    				break;
	    			case 'featuringTemplate':
	    				hmtlContent = `
	    					<div class="featuring">
	    						<div class="featuring-image">
	    							<img src="${content.medium_cover_image}" width="70" height="100" alt="">
	    						</div>
	    						<div class="featuring-content">
	    							<p class="featuring-title">Pelicula encontrada</p>
	    							<p class="featuring-album">${content.title_long}</p>
	    						</div>
	    					</div>
	    				`
	    				break;
	    			default:
	    				hmtlContent = ''
	    		}
	    
	    		const html = document.implementation.createHTMLDocument();
	        	html.body.innerHTML = hmtlContent;
	    
	    		return html.body.children[0];
	    	}
	    
	    	function renderList (list, $elemParent, template, options, category) {
	    		$elemParent.children[0].remove();
	    		list.forEach((content)=>{
	    			content.category = category
	    			const $elementContent = templateContent(template, content)
	    			if (typeof options.fadeIn != "undefined") {
	    				const image = $elementContent.querySelector('img')
	    
	    				image.addEventListener('load', (e)=>{
	    					e.srcElement.classList.add('fadeIn')
	    				})
	    			}
	    
	    			if (options.render === 'html') {	
	    				$elemParent.innerHTML = $elementContent.outerHTML
	    			} else if( options.render === 'append') {
	    				$elemParent.append($elementContent)
	    			}
	    
	    			if (options.click)
	    				addEventClick($elementContent)
	    		})
	    	}
	    	function findById(list, id) {
	    		return list.find(movie => movie.id === parseInt(id, 10))
	    	}
	    
	    	function findMovie(id, category) {
	    		switch (category) {
	    			case 'action' : {
	    				return findById(actionList, id)
	    		}
	    			case 'drama' : {
	    				return findById(dramaList, id)
	    		}
	    			default: {
	    				return findById(animationList, id)
	    			}
	    		}
	    	}
	    	function addEventClick ($element) {
	    		$element.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
	    	      showModal($element)
	    	    })
	    	}
	    
	    	function showModal($element) {
	    		$overlay.classList.add('active')
	    		$modal.style.animation = 'modalIn .8s forwards'
	    		const id = $element.dataset.id;
	    		const category = $element.dataset.category;
	    		const data = findMovie(id, category);
	    
	    		$modalTitle.textContent = data.title
	    		$modalImage.setAttribute('src', data.medium_cover_image)
	    		$modalDescription.textContent = data.synopsis
	    	}
	    
	    	function hideModal() {
	    		$overlay.classList.remove('active')
	    		$modal.style.animation = 'modalOut .8s forwards'
	    	}
	    
	    	/*
	    	** Events on DOM element
	    	*/
	    	$hideModal.addEventListener('click', hideModal)
	    
	    	$form.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
	    		e.preventDefault()
	    		$featuringContainer.innerHTML  =''
	    
	    		$home.classList.add('search-active')
	    
	    		const $loader = document.createElement('img')
	    
	    		setAttributes($loader, {
	    			src: 'src/images/loader.gif',
	    			height: 50,
	    			width: 50
	    		})
	    
	    		$featuringContainer.append($loader)
	    
	    		try { 
	    			const data = new FormData($form)
	    			const {data: {movies}} = await getData(`${API_BASE}/list_movies.json?limit=1&query_term=${data.get('name')}`)
	    			renderList(movies, $featuringContainer, 'featuringTemplate', {click: false, render: 'html'} )
	    		} catch(err) {
	    			console.error(err)
	    			$loader.remove()
	    			$home.classList.remove('search-active')
	    		}
	    	})
	    
	    })()
	    
	```
